name:G‚Äçr‚Äça‚Äçn
info:Deluxe Double Bed Room
info:Stayed in July 2021
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted August 3, 2021
msg:Before this trip, we would not really have thought of ourselves as a "Ritz Carlton" type family.  We like Air BnB's and and finding local places and, well, saving money.

The staff at the Ritz Carlton have ensured our return to this and other properties. Rianna, Richard and Daisy turned our most miserable day into our most memorable day.  

We were finishing our six week holiday around China and had left Xi'an to return to our home in Shanghai.  The train stopped at the first station.  Track problems up ahead (we would find out later that day it was the massive flooding that you've heard about on the news). Minutes turned into hours.  We were stuck for nine hours and sent back to Xi'an.  We scrambled to get a hotel. Everything near the train station and airport was booked. Our young kids were miserable.  Going through trip.com I thought, "Ok, lets do something special for the kids".  Time for putting on the Ritz. 

We get to the hotel and we're greeted by Rianna at the concierge  (I went to the wrong desk) and she kindly guides me to Richard.  Somehow Richard sees that we're totally exhausted and immediately suggests giving us an upgrade.  Wow.  Next we get in the elevator and Rianna escorts us to our room.  She asks if we're here for business or vacation.  I explain that we were on vacation but now we're here because trains aren't leaving the city. I explain its been a rough day.  

We get to our room and I order food from a place nearby.  Becuase my Chinese is so terrible I have it sent to the wrong place.  I'm searching the lobby and Rianna finds me, checks my phone, calls the delivery guy, and then walks me down the street to the mall where I have had my food delivered by accident.  

After dinner, we're getting the kids settled into bed.  Knock at the door.  Rianna and Daisy come in with glasses of warm milk and adorable stuffed animals for the children.  There is also a card from all three of the staff members that says that they hope that our stay has helped us turn the day around.  There was even a hand drawn picture of the four of us on a train and smiling.  It was the most thoughtful gesture I have ever experienced from someone that we had only just met. 

That is how they turned our miserable day into a memorable day.  

The room was amazing and comfortable, the breakfast buffet was delicious and fresh, but the staff was extraordinary.   

Thank you Richard. Thank you Rianna.  Thank you Daisy.   Our summer trip could have ended on a sour note, but because of you, it ended with the happiest of memories. 

Thank you.

msg:Worthy of the title of Ritz-Carlton, it feels the best among the many five-star hotels in Xi'an. Whether it is breakfast, lobby bar, room facilities, or service, they are all impeccable. There is also a high-end shopping mall next to it, where you can eat, drink, and have fun, which complements the Ritz-Carlton, so you don't have to worry about being bored when staying in the hotel. I recommend two places to eat, which are a little far from the Ritz-Carlton, but not far away. One is 3511, where there is a chain store of Xi'an local food Yuanjiacun, as well as various other snacks. Compared with other chain stores, this Yuanjiacun feels more spacious and refreshing, and the taste is also good, it is worth a try. In addition, there is a Tongshengxiang branch of Mutton Soup with Steamed Buns not far away. I often come to Xi'an and will definitely eat Mutton Soup with Steamed Buns. I have eaten in many of them. To be honest, they are all good. I don't feel any difference, including breaking the buns by myself or by machines. They are all almost the same. I guess the resolution of my gourmet cells is not high. So for friends who come and stay in the hotel, if you don't want to join in the crowd and just want to quietly taste the authentic Mutton Soup with Steamed Buns in Xi'an, this one is good. The machine can break the buns. In addition, for friends from other places, when eating steamed buns, it is recommended to tell the waiter to ask for a wider soup, that is, more soup, otherwise friends from other places may not be able to eat it. Finally, I can recommend this store's own sour plum juice.
